Carsten Haase< /name>
<Date>1535066946231</Date><rating>1<//rating>< text>
Edit (addressing owner's response, 8/23/18):
The owner's reply states that "we discussed a course of action to take for the damage". When I took my car back in the next day to tell them about the damage, they seemed willing to pay to get the damage fixed but said were too busy and didn't have any lifts free. They told me to come back the following day so they could look at the damage. The next day I went back, the technician put my car up on one of their lifts, and looked over the damage. After multiple people inspected the damage, they told me it was "superficial" and that "sometimes low cars scrape going up the ramps" so they weren't going to cover it.

This response is too little and 2 months too late. I fixed this myself a long time ago.

6/20/2018:
I hit a large pothole and my alignment slipped enough to make steering wheel crooked when driving in a straight line. Based on all of the positive reviews, I decided to get my car aligned at Dixon Tire Pros. My experience was far from positive.

Making an appointment was easy enough, the waiting room was nice, and the employees were professional. I was told the alignment would take 45 minutes to 1 hour so I decided to wait. It ended up taking 2 hours but they were very busy so the extra time is understandable. Up to this point I was totally satisfied with the service I received.

When I got home I went under my car to mark the alignment cams so I could put them back myself if they slipped again and that's when I noticed the damage. The exhaust was scraped up, there were scratches on the subframe, and the driver's side frame rail was noticeably dented (see picture, the frame rail should be straight along the red line).

I brought my car back in to get them to fix it or at least give me some sort of compensation so I could get it fixed myself but even though they admitted that they damaged the car, they said the damage was "superficial" and that "sometimes low cars scrape going up the ramps". First, just because nothing actually broke and the damage was "superficial" doesn't mean that it is acceptable. What if a door got dented or paint got scratched? Is that superficial damage acceptable? Second, my car has more ground clearance than a Camaro, an Audi S5, and many other cars. If your shop can't handle sports cars then don't offer to work on them!

Dixon Tire Pros may usually have good service when everything goes right but so do a lot of other places. A truly good shop takes care of their customer when things go wrong as well. If you decide to try this place, make sure to take lots of pictures of your car beforehand just in case. I am seriously disappointing in the service I received and would recommend you go somewhere else.<//text>

"Personal services" like waxing are now open, at last...which means I can finally get my brows done regularly (or at least semi-regularly) again!

I understand the staff wants to keep things non-contact as much as possible; which is why they've introduced a new check-in process. Text an "I've arrived!" message to the QR code/phone number on the front door, and the staff will respond when they're clean and ready for your appt. (They do ask that customers don't enter until they've received the confirmation text.)

<rate>5</rate>< review>
I have been recycling here for more than 10 years.  The staff are always friendly and efficient and the owner is always working along side of them, which I think is great. I always try to sort my CRV items before arriving at any recycling center.  This helps the process to be quicker and  less frustrating. The parking area at this location is small so can easily get congested by people parking/sorting where they please. If you fluster or are annoyed easily, like myself, then consider sorting before arriving, as well.</review>

<Time>1600384758172<//Time><rate>5<//rate>< Review>
Been going to this place since 2013.  They stay pretty up to date on their prices, and they can accommodate most anything you bring in.  They used to accept appliances but as of today " 9-17-20 " they no longer accept them.  Separate area for bringing in can and bottles as opposed to heavier loads, so there isn't much of a wait time.  A lot of places are closing down due to Covid and not being able to scrap, but this place has stood strong.   If you have recycling, support your local business and go here.<//Review>

I shopped around a bit and in Newport there is a lot to select from.  Some of these guys state appointments months out and claimed it to be just that busy....come to find out some of these guys are not full time.

So I went to Dr. Bunkis -- who is out of my network, but had really good pictures on his site.  I asked him how many he did and had a full catalog of eyes, plus at-least two of his staffers.  The results looked amazing.  I considered the price difference from in network to out of network, then very quickly  decided on Dr. Bunkis.  Great guy, great personality, and a no BS personality.  The answers were spot on, when I asked about what the Aetna Dr recommended, he quickly pointed out the flaws (ie feminizing the face ---as a guy NOT what I would want).  I also asked about some other body work and he recommended a book by Ornish that gave some fixes via diet --- (actually he gave me his copy) --- It appears to work).

Back to the procedure -- All good the surgical center was next door --- they were nice, and professional, very comfortable.  The Anesthesiologist was easy going.  Everything went as described.  All good.

Dr. Bunkis followed up over the weekend, gave me his cell phone number  for any issues (of which I called and he answered).  I was a bit nervous as after you do a bleph, you get a bit of distorted vision.  Dr. Bunkis put my unease at rest.  And here I  am a few weeks later and my results look day and night better.

The follow ups were little wait and very easy going.  Collette and Jo have been awesome in helping me process the Aetna PPO self claim papers.  Really good guys.

Dr. Bunkis is very approachable and has an amazing story.  I am very glad to have found him and am proud to give an endorsement of him to my friends.

What could have made this better.....Well the office was near perfect.....Aenta on the other hand - not so much......I see why so few would be in there network.  I will also go so far as to say if you are looking in network, the cost savings is not that significant  and I found value with going with someone I indubiously trust.</review>< Pics>

<time>1515887551662<//time><Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
Dr. Bunkis has been my plastic surgeon for nearly 7 years. I met Dr. Bunkis through a friend, who went to him as well for plastic surgery. She couldn't speak highly enough of Orange County Plastic Surgery. I've always gone to him for maintenance (Botox, Juvederm, Laser Treatments). 3 years ago, I had a nose job and a little radio frequency tightening of my jawline. He is one of the only plastic surgeon's in Newport Beach that will do a closed rhinoplasty. He specifically, focused on the tip of my nose as I wanted it a little more refined and less bulbous. It couldn't have turned out better. I was up and around the next day and 3 years later, I think it's still perfect. Nose jobs definitely improve with time as you heal. Recently, I have been feeling that I look tired, getting older, and starting to droop in my eyelids and that my lower face was sagging. I've talked on and off with Dr. Bunkis about having surgery to correct this for 2 years now. The timing was finally right, and after consulting with Dr. Bunkis and Colette, I scheduled a trans-blepharoplasty brow lift and face lift on January 3, 2018. Today is January 10, 2018. I cannot believe it has been 10 days since I had a brow lift and face lift. I went to dinner with my Mother last night. Nobody was staring. We went and ran errands and I felt completely confident being out in public. I got my stitches out a week after my surgery. People will tell you that facial surgery doesn't hurt and that it's a breeze. That's not necessarily true and it depends a lot on which plastic surgeon you choose. I can tell you that his pre-operative and post-operative instructions are almost as critical as the procedures he performs. I had this facelift and brow lift to kind of stop the aging process as I enter a birthday I didn't want to celebrate this year. And I knew that Dr. Bunkis wouldn't leave me looking pulled tight or like a deer caught in the headlights. He takes a very personalized approach when he consults with you. And also will tell you if you shouldn't do something. I find this comforting because he doesn't believe in fixing things that aren't broken.  I told Dr. Bunkis that if I didn't look any better than I did 10 days post-op, that I was as happy as a clam. I truly can't believe how natural and youthful I look. I'm not one to shy away from having plastic surgery to reverse the aging process and I certainly don't mind sharing my experiences going under the knife. What I can tell you is that the first few days of a facelift and brow lift are a little uncomfortable. You've got tubes for drainage on the first day. Which is great, because you don't have all that fluid and blood sitting in your lower face and neck. You are swollen as you would be with any surgery. Ice, ice, ice, and ice some more! Dr. Bunkis also recommended that I sit up at an elevated position when I slept as much as I could and to sleep on my back. Some people won't do that. I can tell you that it's one of the best pieces of advice he gave me for recovery. Yes, it's not ideal to sleep with your head elevated and on your back. But it's so worth it to cut your recovery time literally in half! And it's your FACE! Don't slack and cut corners on his recovery instructions. I did feel tightness around my ears which is normal I think given that's where the stitches are and the muscle is repositioned. I wouldn't say it was painful, rather it felt like pressure that would come and go and dissipated over the first week. 10 days out and I'm slightly numb in a couple of spots, but it's nothing that would prevent me from doing anything I would normally do. If you are thinking about having plastic surgery, without any hesitation I recommend him to family and friends. He doesn't have a one size fits all approach to anything. My Mother has had a facelift, brow lift, upper and lower eyelids, and breast lift with Dr. Bunkis in 2017. She loves her results, too. If you want the best plastic surgeon in Newport Beach, go to Dr. Bunkis! I've never felt more confident. You won't regret it.</review>

< Review>
I've been to this location twice. The first time I came in, I ordered the El Torito Burrito and I was not impressed. The little meat it did have, was hard and flavorless. The pico de gallo was basically just onions, and the guacamole was barely visible. Five months later I came in for another go and I'm glad I did. I ordered the La Torta Cochinita and it was amazing. Very flavorful! The order came with a side of fries which were mediocre, but, honestly the torta was very filling I could have gone without them. The agua frescas are pretty tasty too! And customer service is friendly.< /Review>

<Rating>5< /Rating><review>I contacted them by sending an email via their link on the website home page. This was my first time inquiring about their services and didn't know if I'd get a fairly quick reply or any at all. I was pleased to see a very timely reply to my email saying that my appointment was confirmed for the next morning. It also said I would would receive a call from their driver about 20 min. before they arrived at my address. I had a few items to be picked up by them and was curious about the potential cost so I was pleased to find an 'estimator-type' tool on their webpage. It was easy to use and soon had a rough idea of what I'd be paying. I'd initially planned on loading up my small-bed truck with this stuff to take to the dump but found out it would have quite expensive to 'dump' these items directly at a local place. I figured, heck, it's going to be pricey anyway so I'll see how this Junk King thing works out.
I was glad I did. They called me 20 min into my two-hour appointment window and said they'd be there in about 20-25 min.
